 12:05 AM patidaar aarakshan andolan samiti ke log bharat singh solanki ke ghar pahunche The Narendra Modi government made a historic decision on Monday by giving 10 per cent reservation to the general class on economic grounds
 loksabhaa chunaav se ain pehle sarkaar dwaara aarthik aadhaar par garib savarnon ko sarkari naukari or shiksha ke kshetra main 10 fisadi aarakshan diya gaya
 The opposition has termed the government's decision as just an election bet, while the Bharatiya Janata Party and the government have called it a historic step
 agar aapke man main is faisle se jude kuch sawaal hai to jawaab aapako yahaan milenge
 
 
 1
 savarnon ko aarakshan kiske hisse kaa milegaa?modi sarkaar ne garib savarnon ko jo 10 fisadi aarakshan dene kii baat kahi he, yah aarakshan abhi tak die ja rahe 50 fisadi se alag hoga
 That is, according to the constitution, only 50 percent reservation is given to the backward section of society
 yani sarkaar ne savarnon ko aarakshan dene kaa faisla isse alag diya he, iske liye samvidhan main sanshodhan karnaa hoga
 2
 samvidhan main praavdhaan nahin he phir kaise milegaa?modi sarkaar is faisle ko lagu karne ke liye samvidhan main sanshodhan karegi
 The Constitution amended bill will be introduced in the Lok Sabha on Tuesday itself
 centre sarkaar samvidhan ke anuchhed 15 or anuchhed 16 main badlaav karegi
 Changing both the paragraphs will pave the way for reservation on economic grounds
 3
 Will only the Hindu upper castes get it? It is not at all that the Hindu upper castes will benefit from this decision of the central government
 is faisle kaa laabh hinduon ke alaava muslim or isai dharm ke logon ko bhi milegaa
 For example, if a Muslim falls in the general category and is financially weak, he will get the benefit of 10% reservation
 4
 What will happen to the patel-jat-maratha movement now? In the past, the patel-jat-marathas have made several agitations for reservation
 modi sarkaar ke faislon se inhen bhi laabh milegaa, kyonki ye sabhi jatiyaan savarna ke antargat aati hai
 In such a situation, all these castes will also get 10 per cent benefit on economic basis
 5
 Who will be considered poor and who is not? The Modi government has imposed certain conditions with this decision
 is faisle ke tahat jinaki aay 8 lakh rupee salanaa se kam ho unhen is faisle kaa laabh milegaa, iske alaava jiske paas 5 hectare se kam kii jameen hogi unhen bhi 10 fisadi aarakshan kaa laabh milegaa
 The upper castes having less than 1000 square feet of house, having less than 109 yards of notified land of the corporation, non-notified land of less than 209 yards and all those who do not come under any reservation will be benefited
 will get
 6
 Will the government's bet in the court survive? In fact, according to the constitution, reservation is given only on the basis of social inequality, ie, reservation on economic grounds is non-constitutional
 kai rajya sarkaron ne aarthik aadhaar par aarakshan dene kii koshish kii he, lekin jab maamla court main jaataa he to gaiyr-sanvaidhanik hone ke aadhaar par khaarij kar diya jaataa gaya he
 In such a situation, the challenge will be to amend the constitution before the central government
 7
 Which jobs will get this reservation, center-state or corporations? Modi government will get this benefit in the field of government jobs and education
 modi sarkaar kaa ye faisla puure desh main lagu hoga, aise main jin kshetron main aarakshan kaa praavdhaan he usamen centre-rajya or nigam kii naukari main is faisle kaa laabh sidhe taur par milegaa
 8
 kya rajya bhi de sakenge aisa aarakshan?pichley kuch samay main rajya sarkaron ne jab bhi aarthik aadhaar par aarakshan dene kii koshish kii he to court ne use gaiyrkanoonee qaraar diya he
 In such a situation, if the constitution is amended now, then it may open the way for state governments to give 50 percent separate reservation
 mandal kamishan se savarna aarakshan tak, padhein desh main aarakshan kii timelinekya chunaav se pehle lagu ho paaegaa savarna aarakshan? ye he samvidhan sanshodhan bill kii puri prakriya Saina Nehwal, the only Indian to challenge Chinese dominance in badminton, hopes that her London Olympic bronze medal will inspire at least half a dozen players to reach the top level with her and challenge the traditional powerhouse

 ) The famous Urdu poet Anwar Jalalpuri has died
 vah kareeb 70 varsh ke the
 He breathed his last at the Trauma Center in Lucknow on Tuesday morning
 unke parivaar main teen bete or patni he
 He translated the Gita into Urdu
 jalalpuri ke bete shaahakaar ke anusaar, jalalpuri ko gat 28 disambar ko unke ghar main mastishk aghat ke baad king jorge chikitsa vishvavidhyalay ke troma centre main bhartee karaayaa gaya tha, jahaan subah kareeb sava nau baje unhone antim saans lee
 In 2015, he was awarded the Best Yash Bharti Award in Uttar Pradesh
 jalalpuri ko guuruuvaar dopaher main johar kii namaaj ke baad ambedkar nagar sthit unke paitruk sthal jalalpur main supurd-e-khaak kiya jayega
